 Mirza Ghalib is a great poet of Urdu, who must have heard the name of everyone and used his poetry at some point in life
 urdu ke mahaan shairamirzagalib (mirza Ghalib Quotes) kaa janm 27 disambar, 17979 ko hua tha or unka nidhan 15 farvari, 1869 ko hua
 The real name of Mirza Ghalib was Mirza asad-ullah Beg Khan
 mahaan shairamirzagalib kaa janm us daur main hua jab mughal satta kamjor pad rahi thi or mirzagalib (mirza Ghalib) kaajivan bahut hi mushkil halaat main gujara
 But Mirza Ghalib Poetry wrote a poetry that describes the essence of life
 mirzagalib (mirza Ghalib) bollywood (bollywood) or televijan par unke upar zyada kaam nahin hua he
 Sohrab Modi's film 'mirza Ghalib (1954)' in Bollywood was memorable
 televijan par gulzaar (gulzar) kaa tivi serial ‘mirzagalib(1988)' bhi mile kaa pathar he
